# Improvement Roadmap — Master Tracker

**Created:** 2026-06-10 · **Source docs:** `../nyi/improvement-roadmaps/` (00–06, Codex-reviewed)
**Scope:** critical-path spine ≈ 12–16 wks; full backlog ≈ 25–35 engineer-weeks.

How to use this file: work top-to-bottom within a track; tracks B–D unlock as
Track A milestones land. Check items off here; when a milestone gets a real
spec/plan, write it via the normal brainstorming → writing-plans flow, park it
in `specs/`/`plans/`, and link it next to the item. Statuses: `[ ]` not
started · `[~]` in progress · `[x]` shipped.

**Handoff rule:** whenever an item is completed (or meaningfully advanced),
update this tracker (checkbox + status-log line) **and** rewrite
`HANDOFF-improvement-roadmap.md` in the same commit, so any new chat can pick
up by reading the handoff doc alone.

---

## Track A — Platform foundations (4–5.5 wks) → `06-platform.md`

Spine items — everything else depends on these two:

- [x] **A1. Durable job queue + Schedule table** (2–2.5 wks)
  Job table (claim via conditional update, heartbeat, retries, dedupKey,
  type-keyed concurrency) + worker loop + cron-ish Schedule tick.
  Migrate in order: PSI jobs → PDF scans → site-audit page loop → cleanup.
  Old path stays behind a flag until parity proven.
  Specs: `../archive/specs/2026-06-10-durable-job-queue-design.md` ·
  `../archive/specs/2026-06-10-durable-job-queue-phase3-design.md` ·
  Plans: `../archive/plans/2026-06-10-durable-job-queue.md` (Phases 0–1,
  done) · `../archive/plans/2026-06-10-durable-job-queue-phase2.md`
  (close-out + Phase 2, done) ·
  `../archive/plans/2026-06-10-durable-job-queue-phase3.md` (page loop,
  merged PR #53, deployed + production-verified 2026-06-10) ·
  `../archive/plans/2026-06-10-durable-job-queue-phase4.md` (cleanup ticks,
  merged PR #54, deployed + verified 2026-06-10). Spec:
  `../archive/specs/2026-06-10-durable-job-queue-phase4-design.md`.
  **DONE** — all four phases shipped and production-verified.
- [x] **A2. Normalized findings layer** (2–3 wks)
  `CrawlRun` / `CrawlPage` / `Finding` / `Violation`; dual-write from parse +
  ADA runners; blobs demoted to archive columns; validate parity on 3–5
  representative clients before any reader flips.
  Spec: `../archive/specs/2026-06-10-findings-layer-design.md` (Codex ×10 fixes) ·
  Plan (Phase 1): `../archive/plans/2026-06-10-findings-layer-phase1.md` (Codex ×8
  fixes) — **Phase 1 merged (PRs #55 + #56), deployed, production-verified
  2026-06-10** (PARITY OK on 2 real sessions; cross-run SQL queries working).
  Plan (Phase 2): `../archive/plans/2026-06-10-findings-layer-phase2.md` (Codex ×5
  fixes) — **Phase 2 merged (PR #57), deployed, production-verified
  2026-06-10** (PARITY OK on 2 site audits + 1 standalone).
  DB-growth projection run 2026-06-10 (gated-decisions item: done for A2's
  purposes; C2 must add cadence-aware retention before nightly fleet scans).
  Plan (Phase 3): `../archive/plans/2026-06-11-findings-layer-phase3.md` (Codex ×4
  fixes) — **Phase 3 merged (PR #58), deployed, production-verified
  2026-06-11** (fresh-run parity gate passed on 4 live parses + fresh site
  audits + 1 standalone; SessionPage reader flipped with legacy fallback;
  SessionPage writes stopped).
  Plan (Phase 4): `../archive/plans/2026-06-11-findings-layer-phase4.md`
  (Codex clean accept) — **Phase 4 shipped 2026-06-11**:
  `pruneArchivedBlobs()` 90-d blob retention registered in `runCleanup()`,
  INERT (`PRUNE_ACTIVATED` both `false`; each flag flips in the same PR as
  that tool's last blob reader); CLAUDE.md findings-layer docs; A2 docs
  archived. **A2 COMPLETE.** (`SessionPage` model drop stays a post-A2
  follow-up, ≥180 d after the 2026-06-11 flip.)

Interleave as needed (not blockers):

- [x] A2-f1 (follow-up, added 2026-07-02). **Guard `scripts/findings-rebuild.ts` against pruned ADA blobs** — the Session branch refuses a pruned blob (`findings-rebuild.ts:44-46`) but the SiteAudit/AdaAudit branches have no guard: on a 90-d-pruned ADA row, `parseAxe(null)` yields empty pages and the delete-and-recreate writer silently replaces the canonical findings tables with an empty run. ~5-line guard mirroring the Session check. Found by the 2026-07-02 skill-library factual review; warning documented in `.claude/skills/er-seo-tools-proof-and-analysis-toolkit` until fixed. (hours) — **BUILT + PR #88 (2026-07-02).** Guard placed in `lib/findings/ada-write.ts` (both `writeAdaSiteFindings` + `writeAdaSingleFindings`), NOT the script — defends the rebuild script AND the live standalone dual-write hook. Pruned signature = `status='complete'` audit/child with null `result` (finalizer never persists a complete audit without its blob); errored/redirected audits stay ungated. 2 DB-backed tests (refuse + no-clobber, site + standalone). Gate-green. **MERGED (PR #88, main `92d10e3`) + DEPLOYED (2026-07-02, code-only `~/deploy.sh`, no migration) + PROD-VERIFIED to the extent possible: deployed guard source present in `lib/findings/ada-write.ts`, clean boot, app online. Behavioral rebuild-refuses check DEFERRED — prod has 0 pruned targets (oldest complete ADA audit 41 d old; prune at 90 d), forcing one would mutate prod; guard is correctly inert until the first pruned-audit rebuild (~2026-08+). Behavioral correctness covered by the 2 gate-green DB tests. A2-f1 COMPLETE.**

  `spanClass()` span utilities (`col-span-1`/`md:col-span-2`/`lg:row-span-2`/
  `lg:col-span-4`) live only in `lib/widgets/grid.ts`, but Tailwind's `content`
  globs scanned only `app`/`components`/`pages` — so those classes were **purged
  from the prod CSS since PR 2** (every tile rendered 1-column; unnoticed because
  PR 2's sizing was never eyeballed). Fix = add `./lib/**` to the content globs +
  a guard test; before/after proven by CSS grep (`.md:col-span-2` NOT-FOUND →
  present). —
  the widget editor: pure layout reducer spine (`lib/widgets/layout.ts` —
  normalize/load/serialize/reorder/move/cycle/reducer, never imports the
  registry, never mutates inputs) + hydration-safe `useHomeLayout` hook (SSR +
  first-paint render DEFAULT_LAYOUT; localStorage read only in an effect;
  persist armed only post-hydration — proven via `setItem` call-history +
  StrictMode tests) + `EditableWidgetTile` (drag handle, size stepper, ↑/↓
  keyboard reorder, live body suppressed in edit mode) + stateful
  `DashboardGrid` (Customize/Done/Reset, native HTML5 DnD reorder + trailing
  drop zone, CSS-gated desktop-only). Order+size only; `localStorage(
  'er-home-layout')` = `{version:1,items:[{id,size}]}`; unknown ids dropped,

Ordering: isolation → consolidation → streaming (consolidation shrinks streaming's blast radius; streaming last on the clean base — no active OOM, latent risk only). **Part 3 (streaming parse) MERGED (PR #95, `75b84f6`) + DEPLOYED + PROD-VERIFIED 2026-07-03.** Converts the 4 big-file parsers (externallinks/anchortext/images/linksissues) to row-by-row streaming via a new `StreamingParser` sibling base + `streamCsv` (Papa `NODE_STREAM_INPUT`); route detects filename-first with a bounded header-peek so unmatched files (all_inlinks 7.3MB, external_all) are never fully read. `InternalParser` deferred (small file, O(URLs) state). Byte-identical proven 3 ways: golden characterization (green through refactor) + generic Papa string-vs-stream parity table + real-crawl `deepStrictEqual` vs pre-refactor baselines (all 3 byte-identical). **Key prod-only catch (via the parity table): `Papa.parse(string)` strips a leading UTF-8 BOM but `NODE_STREAM_INPUT` does NOT — every real SF export starts with a BOM that would break `findColumn(['Address','URL'])`; `streamCsv` now strips it.** `streamCsv` resolves on readable `'end'` (never `'finish'`) + rejects on any stream error.   - [x] **INVESTIGATE: scoring-v2 scorecard shows "0 rules passed – 0 needs
    review" on the Bellus audit** — **ROOT-CAUSED (prod-verified): NOT a UI or
    mapper bug.** axe-core's `no-passes` reporter (in `runner.ts` since the
    first browser-runner commit) internally forces `resultTypes=['violations']`,
    silently stripping BOTH `passes` and `incomplete` from every stored blob —
    so all pass/needs-review counts were 0 fleet-wide AND scoring-v2's
    `incompletePenalty` NEVER fired in production (its K=14 calibration
    assumed it did). Fix (PR #141, Codex accept-with-named-fixes ×6): reporter
    `'v2'` + in-page `trimAxeResultsForStorage` (passCount scalar, passes/
    inapplicable dropped pre-serialization, incomplete kept + node-capped);
    all 5 readers prefer the scalar; **ADA_SCORE_VERSION 2→3** (same formula,
    repaired input — at DOM_FLOOR 6 incomplete rules move 100→≈54, so
    cross-version sparkline deltas are suppressed). Legacy blobs keep 0s (data
    never existed) — **a domain needs one fresh scan post-2026-07-09 to show
    real counts** (the in-flight 2026-07-09 Bellus audit is mixed: pages ≤368
    old-shape, the rest new-shape with passCount ≈31/page).

Options: **(a)** deploy.sh runs `pm2 stop seo-tools` BEFORE `npm run build` (server-owned file — Kevin edit; costs ~3–4 min planned downtime per deploy), or **(b)** disable the redundant server-side type-check/lint in `next.config.ts` (`typescript.ignoreBuildErrors` + `eslint.ignoreDuringBuilds` — already gated by local tsc + tests before every merge). **DECIDED 2026-07-11 (Kevin): option (b). - 2026-07-06 (PR #107 adversarial review → safeFetch hardening PR #108 — Kevin-requested review, small-fix class) — **#107 REVIEWED (8 finder angles, per-finding verify) → #107 is CORRECT; 3 CONFIRMED hardening gaps fixed + shipped (PR #108, `b68a83f`).** (1) The settle invariant in `fetchWithPinnedAddress` was conventional (status checks OUTSIDE the try) — now STRUCTURAL: one `fail()` helper + a callback-wide try/catch; no future callback statement can reopen the never-settling class. (2) Deterministic response-level failures (missing status / out-of-range status / Response-construction throw) now ALL reject `SafeUrlError` → `resolveUrl` stops firing the doomed identical GET retry the raw-error path caused (up to 2× requests/link vs pathological hosts). (3) The LAST never-settling path closed: tarpit host + signal-less caller — `pdf-runner.fetchOnce` passes NO AbortSignal (120s pdf-scan job timeout reclaimed the slot but leaked promise+socket) — fixed with a 30s inactivity-based idle-socket timeout in the transport (slow-but-flowing downloads unaffected; shorter caller signals still win). (4) safeFetch's redirect loop now cancels intermediate responses' unread bodies (sockets were held until the caller's abort). **#107's "real transport isn't loopback-testable" claim was WRONG** — `fetchWithPinnedAddress` does no address validation (that's `resolveSafeHttpUrl`), so it's now exported test-only (createPinnedLookup precedent) with real-transport loopback regression tests: 999 rejects-not-hangs (the incident class), 200 resolves, idle timeout fires, redirect-body cancel. Review verdicts also: REFUTED destroy-before-reject hazard (Node stream `destroy()` can't throw synchronously — ordering unified anyway); NOT actionable: `/api/fetch-url` mapping a 999 to 400 vs 502 (invisible to its only consumer). - 2026-07-04 (C6 hybrid discovery Increment 1 — sitemap miss-rate measurement — merged+deployed+verified) — **Sitemap miss-rate measurement SHIPPED (PR #101, main `9a70368`) + DEPLOYED + PROD-VERIFIED.** Roadmap-menu pick (Kevin: further C6 → hybrid discovery Phase 2). Because the roadmap GATES the full crawler on a never-measured number (§5: "build the crawler only if measurement shows sitemaps routinely miss pages"), Kevin chose a **measurement-first** shape: an increment that produces the miss-rate number from data the audit ALREADY harvests — **depth-1, zero new fetches, no change to the audited page set** — deferring the actual crawler (Increment 2) to an evidence-backed follow-up. **The insight:** the ADA audit already harvests every `<a href>` into `HarvestedLink`; the link-graph builder DISCARDS targets outside the audited set (`link-graph.ts:20`) — those discarded same-domain internal-link targets ARE the "pages the sitemap missed," one hop out. **What shipped:** (1) pure `computeDiscoveryCoverage` + `normalizeCoverageUrl` (`lib/ada-audit/seo/discovery-coverage.ts`) — diffs coverage-normalized internal-link targets vs the coverage-normalized `SiteAudit.discoveredUrls` baseline; `missRate=|O|/(|B|+|O|)`; excludes images + non-page file extensions; capped source-attributed sample. (2) 3 additive nullable columns (migration `20260704120000_discovery_coverage`): `CrawlRun.discoveryCoverageJson`, `SiteAudit.discoveryMode`, `SiteAudit.discoveryCapped`. (3) `discoverPages` now returns `{urls,mode,capped}` (`capped = deduped.length > HARD_CAP` pre-slice); provenance recorded at every `discoveredUrls` writer (discover handler in the same first-writer-wins updateMany; `enqueueAudit` → `pre-discovered`). (4) builder computes coverage from already-loaded rows (NO new query) + attaches `discoveryCoverageJson` — **NOT a Finding** (a Finding would inflate `priority.service.calculatePriorityScore`, count-0 scale 1.0 — same landmine as C6 external-link). (5) sibling `DiscoveryCoverageSection` (read-time; measured / not-applicable / clean / absent states; headline only when `mode==='sitemap' && !capped`). **Trust gate:** seed-url clients stay `pre-discovered` by design (NOT bypassed — bypassing would change the audited set); the campaign's clean measurement population is sitemap-discovered clients (scheduled seoIntent audits w/o seedUrls). - 2026-07-04 (C6 external-link verification — merged+deployed+verified) — **External-link verification SHIPPED (PR #100, main `a421c25`) + DEPLOYED + PROD-VERIFIED.** Roadmap-menu pick (Kevin) — completes C6 broken-link Phase 1 (SF-retirement §5): the live-scan builder previously HARVESTED external `<a href>`/`<img src>` targets but only VERIFIED same-domain internal links/images (one `where` filter dropped externals). Now it verifies externals too. **What shipped:** (1) `parseNonNegativeInt` (`lib/jobs/config.ts`) — `0` is a valid return (kill switch), distinct from `parsePositiveInt`. (2) `resolveExternalHead` (`lib/ada-audit/url-resolver.ts`) — **HEAD-only** external check (never a GET, unlike internal `resolveUrl`'s HEAD→GET); broken = 404/410/5xx, everything else (401/403/405/429 anti-bot, other 4xx, throws) = `unconfirmed`. (3) mapper (`broken-link-mapper.ts`): `TYPE_OF['external-link']`→`broken_external_links` (reuses the SF-world type — priority 35, `external` membership), per-call `severity` param (external `warning`, internal stays `critical`). (4) builder (`broken-link-verify.ts`): an **additive second pass** over `external-link` rows — separate query/`externalBroken` array/`externalCache`, so the **internal pass is byte-unchanged**; own cap `BROKEN_LINK_EXTERNAL_MAX_CHECKS` (default 300, **0 disables**), **remaining-time-aware** soft budget `BROKEN_LINK_EXTERNAL_TIME_BUDGET_MS` (default 300000, clamped by `JOB_TIMEOUT_MS − elapsed − SAFETY_RESERVE_MS(60s)`), shorter timeout `BROKEN_LINK_EXTERNAL_TIMEOUT_MS` (8000); worker try/catch wraps BOTH `throttle.wait` + `resolveExternal` (a throw degrades one target to `unconfirmed`, never a job-fail/retry loop); `externalCapped||externalHarvestTruncated` flips the run to `partial`. (5) UI (`BrokenLinksSection.tsx`): amber **warning tier** below the red internal tier; per-tier partial/coverage line from each finding's OWN detail; `run.status` partial note on the clean state. **NO zero-count finding** — plan review caught that a count-0 `broken_external_links` would inflate `priority.service.calculatePriorityScore` (count-0 scale defaults 1.0 → nonzero); coverage transparency comes from `run.status` instead (the alternative spec-Codex #10 offered). - 2026-07-04 (streaming concurrency — C7 Phase-3 payoff — merged+deployed+verified) — **Streaming parse concurrency SHIPPED (PR #99, main `47c5f87`) + DEPLOYED + PROD-VERIFIED.** Roadmap-menu pick (Kevin) — the C7 Phase-3 payoff, unblocked by C7 pt3 streaming (bounded per-file memory is the precondition the roadmap required: "don't parallelize parsing before streaming it"). **What shipped:** `lib/parsers/parse-limit.ts` (new) — a `Semaphore` FIFO counting primitive, `parseConcurrencyFromEnv` (clamps bad/0/negative/**NaN**→2), `PARSE_CONCURRENCY` (default 2), and `mapWithConcurrency<T,R>(items, fn)` = a per-call worker pool over a **single process-wide** `Semaphore(PARSE_CONCURRENCY)` (returns results in INPUT order; caps total concurrent parses across ALL simultaneous uploads — chosen over per-request so two analysts uploading at once can't stack 2N big-file streams against the 2400M ceiling). `app/api/parse/[sessionId]/route.ts`: the sequential `for...of await parseOne(...)` loop swapped for `mapWithConcurrency(sessionFiles, parseOne)` + an ordered collection over the input-ordered `outcomes` — **everything from aggregator ingestion onward is byte-unchanged** (the load-bearing ordering invariant: `mergeParserData` has order-sensitive latest-wins/domain-tally branches, so ingestion must stay in `sessionFiles` order → identical aggregated output, only faster). Math.floor(size) : 1` + a clamp-coverage test (TDD: NaN case timed out pre-fix). Plan doc synced to both corrections.   default). Fix: `experimental.middlewareClientMaxBodySize: '100mb'` in `next.config.ts` (matches the

  deployed, clean boot. **Next: roadmap choice** (C7 / C9 / further C6, or SF-retirement Phase 1).

  audit/child with a null `result` blob is the 90-d-prune signature (the finalizer

  and `writeAdaSingleFindings` throw before the delete-and-recreate writer runs.

  freshly-completed audit always has its blob). Errored/redirected audits are

NEW: terminal Job-row retention (`lib/jobs/retention.ts`, complete/cancelled 7 d / error 30 d, raw-SQL with slot-record guard protecting `Schedule.lastJobId` + current `(scheduleId, nextRunAt)` slots) added to `runCleanup()`. Spec + plan each Codex-reviewed (accept-with-fixes ×5 / ×4, all applied). 22 new tests; suite 1,726 green (164 files); tsc + build green. Next: merge/deploy + post-deploy schedule verification, then A1 → `[x]`.
- 2026-06-10 — **A1 Phase 2 merged (PR #51), deployed, and VERIFIED in production** — after one real incident: the first PDF-bearing audit wedged with SQLite "Operations timed out" (audit failed 15/23 pages). Root cause: interactive `$transaction(async tx =>)` holds SQLite's write lock across event-loop round-trips; 4 concurrent pdfjs parses starve the loop; the lock outlives `busy_timeout` and all writers time out. Fix (PR #52, deployed): all three interactive transactions (PSI settle, PDF settle, PDF insert) converted to array-form with SQL `EXISTS` conditional counter bumps + manual `updatedAt`; rule added to CLAUDE.md "Do not". Verification: identical audit (nyinstituteofmassage.com, 23 pages, 11 PDFs) completed in 59s with 0 timeouts; **Test A** restart mid-`pdfs-running` with an in-flight durable pdf-scan job → "resuming audit … (1 durable job(s) outstanding)", PDF re-scanned, audit finalized 11/11; **Test B** drained `pdfs-running` parent with zero jobs → "finalized drained audit" (finalize-before-fail works in prod). 1,679 tests green. Next: Phase 3 (page loop).
